Methods

get: /albums
AlbumProfileMedia
albumsGet Retrieve list of albums.

Parameters

accessToken (required)
Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
type (required)
Query Parameter — type of the entity of the album.
entity (required)
Query Parameter — identifier of the entity of the album.

Return type

AlbumResponse

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "message" : "aeiou",
  "body" : [ {
    "isDefault" : true,
    "name" : "aeiou",
    "mediaCount" : 123,
    "description" : "aeiou",
    "photo" : {
      "defaultPhoto" : true,
      "width" : 123,
      "id" : 123,
      "url" : "aeiou",
      "thumbnailUrl" : "aeiou",
      "height" : 123
    },
    "id" : 123
  } ]
}

Return type

    "url" : "aeiou",
    "thumbnailUrl" : "aeiou",
    "height" : 123
  },
  "id" : 123
}

get: /clubs
ClubManagement

Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
userId (required)
Query Parameter — The user's identification number
filter (required)
Query Parameter — Could be manage or belongTo.

Return type

get: /clubs/{club_id}/teams
ClubManagement
clubsClubIdTeamsGet Retrieve info of all the teams (along with it's division, season and competition) of a club.

Parameters

clubId (required)
Path Parameter — Identifier of the club you want to get details.
accessToken (required)
Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
findLastOnly (required)
Query Parameter — Flag that helps to know if you want to retrieve only the info of the last season the teams are playing in. Set to false if you want to retrieve the info of all seasons the teams.

Return type

ClubTeam

post: /comments/{comment_id}/likes
PostsAndFeeds
commentsCommentIdLikesPost Like/Up/Down a comment &#9989;

Parameters

accessToken (required)
Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
commentId (required)
Path Parameter — The identification number of a comment.
reactionType (required)
Query Parameter — Reaction type: up, down or like.

Return type

LikeResponse

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "message" : "aeiou",
  "body" : "{}"
}

get: /events/search
EventsSearch
eventsSearchGet Search for events: games, practices, meetings, pickups or all together.

Parameters

accessToken (required)
Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
eventType (required)
Query Parameter — Filter by type of event: all, Game, Practice or Meeting
date (required)
Query Parameter — Provide a starting datetime by which to filter events using UTC timezone. Format ISO-8601: 2015-02-25T17:53:03Z
endDate (optional)
Query Parameter — Define the end datetime of the interval using UTC timezone. Format ISO-8601: 2015-02-25T17:53:03Z. (By default, adds 24 hours to date)
limit (required)
Query Parameter — Maximum number of returned events. (Default 25, maximum 100)
playing (optional)
Query Parameter — If true only return currently playing games
professional (optional)
Query Parameter — If true only return professional games
team (optional)
Query Parameter — Identifiers of the teams you want to search for. You can pass multiple teams separated by commas: 12,3,4 etc.
competition (optional)
Query Parameter — Identifiers of the competitions you want to search for. You can pass multiple competitions separated by commas: 12,3,4 etc.
season (optional)
Query Parameter — Identifiers of the seasons you want to search for. You can pass multiple seasons separated by commas: 12,3,4 etc.
division (optional)
Query Parameter — Identifiers of the divisions you want to search for. You can pass multiple divisions separated by commas: 12,3,4 etc.

Return type

EventResponse

Parameters

eventTimeline (optional)
Query Parameter — Filter based on if the event is a past, upcoming or current event
limit (optional)
Query Parameter — Maximum number of returned events. (Default 25, maximum 100)
start (optional)
Query Parameter — Record to start listing at
following (optional)
Query Parameter — Only return the schedule of the teams followed by the logged in user
includeToday (optional)

eventsUsersUserIdCalendarViewGet Get user events for calendar view &#9989;

Parameters

accessToken (required)

startDate (required)
Query Parameter — Start date of interval. UTC Format ISO-8601: 2015-02-25
endDate (optional)
Query Parameter — end date of interval. UTC Format ISO-8601: 2015-02-25 (By default, 24H day after start)
userEvents (optional)
Query Parameter — True to return user events
childrenEvents (optional)
Query Parameter — True to return children events
favoritesEvents (optional)
Query Parameter — True to return favorites events
eventType (optional)

get: /events/users/{user_id}/invites
Events
eventsUsersUserIdInvitesGet List all the events, according to the event type, the user has. &#9989;

Parameters

accessToken (required)
Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
userId (required)
Path Parameter — User unique identifier.
eventType (required)
Query Parameter — Type of the events you want to retrieve. By default is all. (You can retrieve a combinations of event by separating them by commas, example 'Game,Practice')
eventTimeline (required)
Query Parameter — Filter based on if the events is past or upcoming
limit (optional)
Query Parameter — Max number of elements to retrieve. By default is 20.
start (optional)
Query Parameter — Record to start listing at. By default is 0.
status (optional)
Query Parameter — The type of rsvp status you want to retrieve. By default is all

Return type

EventResponse

get: /events/users/{user_id}/next_up
Events
eventsUsersUserIdNextUpGet List Next Up events for a user &#9989;

Parameters

accessToken (required)
Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
userId (required)
Path Parameter — User's identification number.
date (optional)
Query Parameter — date to search event for. UTC Format ISO-8601: 2015-02-25
userEventsLimit (optional)
Query Parameter — limit the number of user_events returned
eventType (optional)
Query Parameter — Filter by type of event: All, Game, Practice, Pickup or Meeting, Use a CVS string including one or more of these types to get the respective types.
favoritesOnly (optional)
Query Parameter — Only return events for user, favorites teams and favorites leagues and the list of all the competition (but without events)
competition (optional)
Query Parameter — Filter by competition (only return events for this specific competition)

Return type

NextUpEventsResponse

get: /me/invites
Events
meInvitesGet List all the events, according to the event type, the user has. &#9989;

Parameters

accessToken (required)
Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
eventType (required)
Query Parameter — Type of the events you want to retrieve. By default is all. (You can retrieve a combinations of event by separating them by commas, example 'Game,Practice')
eventTimeline (required)
Query Parameter — Filter based on if the events is past or upcoming
limit (optional)
Query Parameter — Max number of elements to retrieve. By default is 20.
start (optional)
Query Parameter — Record to start listing at. By default is 0.
status (optional)
Query Parameter — The type of rsvp status you want to retrieve. By default is all

Return type

EventResponse

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "message" : "aeiou",
  "body" : [ {

Parameters

Query Parameter — The type restricts the search domain to a team, competition, page, group, etc. Use a CVS string including one or more of these types to indicate a search over the respective types. get: /posts
PostsAndFeeds
postsGet Lists postings for a user, team or competition.

Parameters

accessToken (required)
Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
type (required)
Query Parameter — The type can be of value User, Competition, CompetitionNews, CompetitionRoom, Team, Me, TeamRoom, Game, Pickup, Practice, Meeting or Venue.
id (optional)
Query Parameter — If type is me, ID is not required, otherwise the identification number of the type's entity.
beforeDate (optional)
Query Parameter — Collect posts before this date. (ISO-8601 UTC. E.g: 2015-02-25 or 2015-02-25T17:53:03Z)
beforeId (optional)
Query Parameter — Collect posts before the post with this id
filterBy (optional)
Query Parameter — Filter by All, Post, Commentary, Article. To add multiple filters, combine comma delimited, e.g.: Post,Commentary
publicOnly (optional)
Query Parameter — Don't return posts made by the profile, e.g.: For Team A posts, don't return post made by Team A

Return type

PostsResponse

post: /posts/videos
PostsAndFeeds
postsVideosPost Create a post (new format)

Parameters

accessToken (required)
Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
type (required)
Query Parameter — The type can be of value User, Competition, Team, TeamRoom, CompetitionRoom, Feed, Game, Pickup, Practice, Meeting or Venue
id (required)
Query Parameter — The unique identifier of the specified entity type.
privacy (required)
Form Parameter — privacy level
title (optional)
Form Parameter — title - used for article
subtitle (optional)
Form Parameter — subtitle - used for article
postAsType (required)
Form Parameter — Post as type (User, Team, Competition and self). If type is self then postAsEntity is null.
postAsEntity (required)
Form Parameter — The identification number of the postAsType.
content (optional)
Form Parameter — The identification number of the postAsType.
targetLanguage (optional)
Form Parameter — Language of the post.
tagged (optional)
Form Parameter — The entities that are tagged in a post e.g. [{\"id\":\"34\",\"type\":\"Team\"}]
assets (optional)
Form Parameter — The assets that are past (shared: Post or Event) e.g. [{\"entity\":63990,\"type\":\"Post\"}]
fileData (optional)
Form Parameter — Base64 image to upload
linkUrl (optional)
Form Parameter — Url pointing to a video on Youtube or Vimeo e.g. {\"description\":\"test desc\",\"img\":\"http://cdn.sstatic.net/\", \"imgType\":\"small\",\"provider\":null,\"title\":\"title \",\"type\":\"link\", \"url\":\"http://stackoverflow.com\", \"videoId\":null}
videoUrl (optional)
Form Parameter — Url pointing to a video on Youtube or Vimeo
video (optional)
Form Parameter — The video file, can be more than one video, the name must be like video=value1, video=value2, video=value3 also can be used like videox=value1, videoy=value2, video=value3... Max video size 100MB

Return type

Status

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "error" : {
    "code" : 123,
    "devMessage" : "aeiou",
    "message" : "aeiou"
  },
  "message" : "aeiou",
  "body" : [ "aeiou" ]
}

get: /search
Search
searchGet Search for a team, player, venue, competition or event. Depending on the specified type extended filters are available &#9989;

Parameters

accessToken (required)
Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
term (required)
Query Parameter — Search term.
type (optional)
Query Parameter — The type restricts the search domain to a team, player, venue, competition, etc. Use a CVS string including one or more of these types to indicate a search over the respective types. Omitting the type query parameter will indicate a search over all types.
limit (optional)
Query Parameter — Limit the amount of results that are sent back. (defaults to 25, maximum 100)
limited (optional)
Query Parameter — Set to true to limit the search to non professional entities
professionalOnly (optional)
Query Parameter — Set to true to limit the search to professional entities
teamRoomEntity (optional)
Query Parameter — The id of the team room, if the search will happen on a team room

Return type

SearchResponse

Example data

put: /users/{user_id}/profile
ParentingManagement
usersUserIdProfilePut As a parent (or child), I want to edit my child (or parent) user information &#9989;

Parameters

accessToken (required)
Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
userId (required)
Path Parameter — Unique identifier of the user. If the user who will be performing the request is the parent, you have to pass the kid_id. Otherwise pass the parent_id.
body (required)
Body Parameter — Profile definition.

Return type

Status

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "error" : {
    "code" : 123,
    "devMessage" : "aeiou",
    "message" : "aeiou"
  },
  "message" : "aeiou",
  "body" : [ "aeiou" ]
}
get: /users/{user_id}/relations
ParentingManagement
usersUserIdRelationsGet As a parent (or child), I want to see my parenting passbook. (Retrieves all the children or parents of the user you specify)

Parameters

accessToken (required)
Query Parameter — In order to make authorized calls to PlayerPro's APIs, your application must first obtain an OAuth access token.
userId (required)
Path Parameter — Unique identifier of the user.
start (optional)
Query Parameter — offset of the search. (by default is 0)
limit (optional)
Query Parameter — max number of items to retrieve. (by default is 25)

Return type

array[RelationSummary]

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
[ "" ]
